<Review>Like many recent visitors I have been concerned for Ruth Lake and all its citizens. After asking how everyone was doing after the fire, I came to an overwhelming conclusion that it is a lot worse than it should have been. Many homes were lost and most of the forest burnt because of a poor response, interference and bickering by agencies about who gets to put out what fire and whos homes were most important to save. It was a very sad day when I learned that it was decided to just let homes burn to save an empty campground. What a sad time for the area! It should have all been able to be saved. What has been happening to this small community after is also terrible. Tensions are running high and citizens are still being mistreated.</Review><pictures>None< /pictures>< Resp>

< text>
I drove over 12 hours in one day to get to Ruth Lake Campground from Carson, CA. It was a long but super easy drive and it was well worth the mileage. This campground is amazing. We arrived at 5:30 am, just in time for a gorgeous sunrise over the mountains and water. We went fishing right away in the calm, quiet waters. Everyone seemed to be catching fish so easily. Our campsite was right next to the lake. The feeling of waking up & walking outside of your tent to a view of the trees, lake & wildlife here is one of the greatest feelings. The bathrooms were clean, nothing fancy but very nice to have close by. They also offer 5 minute showers for $1, which was well worth it. The campgrounds are clean, spacious and very quiet. I will definitely be returning here, hopefully soon. The highlight of my trip, besides the clean lake, was the giant American Bald Eagle that showed up moments before we were leaving. Priceless.<//text>

<Text>Dr. Stacey Quo has treated both of my daughters for the last 3 years for their misaligned teeth. This was a complete surprise as I taken my children to see Dr. Quo thinking she was just going to help straighten their teeth.  We took Dr. Quo's advice and after having sleep studies, both of my kids were diagnosed with sleep apnea.  Thank goodness she observed this problem because even their Pediatrician did not recommend any additional studies despite their allergy symptoms and delayed growth.  Two and a half years after beginning their sleep apnea treatment, both of my kids have few to no allergy symptoms and are back on the growth chart!  Her expertise in orthodontics is unsurpassed and her knowledge of these other medical conditions as they relate to the mouth and jaw are incredible. Easy place to lose track of time. I come when the lights are on and stay well into  them turning the lights off. Bowling and pool is a beautiful combination. The crowd that comes here keeps the venue exciting. The later into the day you stay the wilder it gets. It‚Äôs a party up in here. I always have a lot of fun when I visit. The competition really shows up here.  It‚Äôs all fun and games until someone bowls a 279

I‚Äôve been practicing and I‚Äôm considering joining a league soon. People come at all skill levels, but I see a bunch of great bowlers here regularly. Sweet place to be at during the week or on the weekend. Can‚Äôt go wrong.< /Review>

<Rate>4< /Rate>< text>
I have not been here in years but this place is just as good as I remember. They even added a lift for the handicapped individuals who want to bowl and I thought that was cool. This place is welcoming and you really have no reason not to have a good time here, unless you're by yourself. They also have billiards and arcade games here as well. The food is what you would expect. The public prices are reasonable, and some of the shoe rentals are very old and some are newer but both work. There were plenty of bowling balls when I went but if multiple Lanes were filled there might've been a shortage but not by much. I also observed that the scoring was a bit off at times. We brought a child and he was able to use the bumper lane and the other bowling helper. I am glad that I finally made it back to this alley.<//text>

<userid>114569660642360341455</userid><user_name>Chris Bach</user_name><time>1423675479601< /time><rating>5< /rating>< Review>
I have to give Jeff 5 stars; it's a small store and the sign to find it is small, but the place has the right spirit, and Jeff was super helpful.  His prices were totally fair, too.  Walked out with about 7 @ 99 cents (some Heart in there, for example!), ZZ Top Fandango and Eliminator @ $3.99/ea (both in good shape), Missing Persons Spring Session M (hard to find) @ $3.99, and the mint prize of the day, a just received ZZ Top Tres Hombres in Mint Condition for $10.  I had him throw in Heart Bad Animals (which was $3.99, but he admitted was not a popular album), and a 99 cent piece which I was on the fence on cause of a scratch over one track..

They have two listening stations, but one is under the neon sign so there's an inductive ground loop audible in the headphones, use the station on the right, further back.

Place is tucked in a wonderful town which I visit regularly for business (have driven by this place 50+ times and never would've known it was there were it not for the front desk at the TownePlace down the street who noticed me bringing a haul of records into the room).  Is just on the fringe of downtown, next to restaurant row (before the basketball courts/park/trails, connected to some closed industrial buildings, not the best in lighting at night).

Parking would be a pain were it not for the driveway on the side of the building serving closed businesses, so I just put the truck right there.  So glad I stopped.  Will be back.  Thank you for what you do, Jeff</Review>

< Text>
Love that chicken at Popeyes. I came to this location at 3 separate occasions, all the times I came to this specific Popeyes, they are out of items that keep them in business such as butter, biscuits, chicken breast, mashed potatoes, hot sauce, etc. I can go on. 1st visit they were out of mild chicken tenders, so I got the spicy tenders. It took  least 20 mins (this is fast food) to get my order and the chicken tenders were extra salty and weren't even temperature hot. The 2nd visit the staff were unorganized and almost gave me the wrong order, not to mention that the employee in the back was on their cell phone I should have cancelled my order and never returned. The 3rd visit chicken was cold, the buscuits were burnt, the Mac and cheese was like mashed potatoes mushy, the Cole slaw was warm, the pies were ok. The customer service is the worst, they forget items like your chicken, your sides, biscuits etc. So i call the number to explain what I'm missing, and no answer. After several attempts a young woman answers the phone I tell her what items I'm missing, she was semi polite and gets my order number and offers me to get my missing items replaced. So I arrive and I tell the cashier that I called and my order was incorrect. I waited for about 20mins for them to replace the items. No extra anything for their fault and making me drive to get the items that they forgot to input my order. I would be a shame to have the employees they have, Popeyes should be and would be if they see the conditions and the way these employees conduct themselves. The cashier was rolling her eyes when I told her their dilemma, the on site supervisor didn't applogize for any inconvenience. It seems that they hire kids with no experience and they don't care about the owners business, I swear that these kids have their friends come by to eat for free, I guess this is the owners problem if they expect to stay in business. I'm surprised they are still in business. I refuse to be a customer at this location ever.<//Text>
